Electronic records must contain detailed information about income, own consumption and sale or transfer of a mineral oil comprising document numbers, numbers, notification of the acquisition to the tax authorities, the place of storage and of consumption, the purpose of consumption, the place of storage and consumption, or in the sale of place of delivery and the registration number of the customer.
Notice of any acquisition of a special mineral oil must be to the tax administrator made in the interval of 24 to 72 hours before admission.
The identification of the trading partners, the name and nomenclature of the special mineral oil, quantity, purpose of consumption or information on sales or transfer shall be notified.
Notification of the estimated amount in the respective year acquired, sold or consumed mineral oil presents the body together with the application for registration or by the end of January of the relevant calendar year.
Notification of the purpose of use and tagging, a place of storage or consumption, the identification data of the person, which is a special mineral oil further sold or transferred, shall be transmitted prior to any change.
Notifications are submitted electronically through smart forms or through a Data Box in PDF format.
In 2015, specialty mineral oils filed 630 notifications.
Seizure and confiscation of the specific mineral oils, or of the means of transport must tax say in cases where he finds dealing with special mineral oils without the registration or when a registered person fails to comply with its reporting obligation.
As in the case of non-compliance with obligations in the transport of excise products, these deficiencies cannot be corrected additionally.
Registration of a fuel distributor is mandatory for persons who sell or are authorized to sell fuel.
Only persons meeting the following criteria may be registered fuel distributors:
Compulsory concession of the trade authority (specific form of Trade Authorisation).
The application for the concession, where applicable, to the provisions of the responsible representative, gives the opinion of the customs authority, which examines whether the applicant for the concession, statutory body or members of the statutory body of the applicant – legal person and the authorized representative meet the condition of reliability.
Where such persons fulfil the condition of reliability, the customs office shall issue a consenting opinion.
A reliable person means a person of integrity, in terms of criminal property, Customs and tax law.
The condition for issuing the concession is professional competence.
Indebtedness of the same circle of persons as in the case of reliability.
Bezdlužnou person is a person who provides sufficient guarantees that he will properly and timely perform their payment obligations to the state, i.e., does not have arrears to the state budget and on the general health insurance.
The fuel distributor shall not be subject to a prohibition by a court or administrative authority on an activity preventing the exercise of its activity.
The fuel Distributor shall not be in liquidation or bankruptcy.
The composition of the deposit (or bank guarantee) of CZK 20,000,000( i.e. about € 740,000), which can be reduced to CZK 10,000,000 (i.e. about €370,000) after three years of registration of the fuel distributor and other conditions.
Notification of fuel distribution the distributor is obliged to submit to the customs office within 20 days after the end of the calendar month.
The electronic notification shall contain information on the individual purchase and sale of fuel.
Reportable data are data about business partners, numbers of documents, the selected product, quantity, price, carriers and transport, place of loading and unloading.
The right to a refund of the tax on mineral oils consumed in agricultural primary production was reintroduced at the end of 2014.
To claim a refund of excise taxes on mineral oils can be only that activity which is obviously related to the activities carried out on the land.
In 2015 there were about 64 thousand claims for tax refunds totalling CZK 1,172,844,680 (i.e. € 43,401,720).
Since 2017, the government of the Czech Republic has also introduced a refund of excise duty on fuel to farmers with livestock production.
Farmers or breeders who, for example, are engaged in cattle, pigs, poultry, sheep and goats will be able to claim this right.
Tobacco products
Restrictions on the sale of tobacco products with an old tax rate
In response to the long-term underachievement of budgeted excise revenue from tobacco products, the Czech Republic introduced effective from 1. 12. 2014 restrictions on the sale of tobacco products with the old tax rate in the event of a change in the tax rate.
Excise tax on tobacco products is paid by using tobacco stickers.
The use of a tobacco sticker means its placement on a unit package (section 116 of the excise duty act).
For the use of the rates of excise taxes shall manufacture a tobacco product in the state intended for the final consumer, which may not occur to its removal from storage, delivery, dispatch or sale of, or sale to the ultimate consumer.
Letter of the alphabet characterizing the rate of excise duty is indicated on the tobacco label along with the price for the final consumer of cigarettes, on the sticker it states the number of pieces in the package, or quantity of smoking tobacco in kilograms.
The tobacco sticker has no identifier.
The length of the transitional period for the sale of unit packets of cigarettes, intended for direct consumption and bearing a tobacco label, with the previous (old) tax rate was established until the expiry of the last day of the second calendar month after the effectiveness of the new rates of excise duty.
From the development of the harvesting of tobacco stamps in 2014 and the comparison with developments in previous years shows that manufacturers of tobacco products each year significantly předzásobili tobacco products with the "old" rate of tax, thereby causing an effective shift of the efficiency of the "new" tax rates by approximately one year.
Raw tobacco tax
Because of the abuse of raw tobacco to manufacturing tobacco products without a warrant, the tax administrator and the non-payment of the excise tax was as a measure against tax fraud introduced a tax on raw tobacco and monitoring the handling of raw tobacco.
Effective from 1. 7. 2015 shall be subject to the excise tax raw tobacco that has not been used or supplied for the manufacture of tobacco products, supplied to another member state or third country, or which had not been shown the origin, the purpose of the use or person that has been or is to be raw tobacco delivered.
Restrictions on the handling of raw tobacco
Measures, such as supervision and control of shipments and production of tobacco products, marking of unit packing tape and restrictions on the sale of the designated places, has been supplemented by restrictions to dispose of the raw tobacco.
Production facilities for the processing of tobacco raw materials and the production of tobacco products shall not be subject to the supervision of the customs authorities.
Store raw tobacco for any purpose other than for the manufacture of tobacco products may only a registered person, such tobacco shall not be further processed or edited.
The registered person can only be a person fulfilling the personal conditions of the applicant, the statutory body and the responsible representative, which applies throughout the registration period.
The terms and conditions of registration are: a) permission to operate a business allowing the performance of the activities of the person storing the raw tobacco, b) reliability, c) bezdlužnost, d) the fact that the person storing the raw tobacco was not specifically forbidden to the activities preventing the performance of its activities, e) the fact that the person storing the raw tobacco is not in liquidation or in bankruptcy, f) the granting of bail in the amount of 20 000 000 Czk (i.e. about 740 000 €).
Electronic records must include the date of receipt or supply of raw tobacco, the number of the document, identification of the business partner, an indication of the quantity and type of raw tobacco.
Notification of any acquisition of raw tobacco by a registered person storing raw tobacco shall be made to the tax authority at an interval of 24 to 72 hours prior to receipt or dispatch.
Information on the business partner, quantity of raw tobacco, storage address, purpose of Use and carrier data shall be reported.
Notification of the estimated amount in the relevant year received or sent raw tobacco presents the body together with the application for registration or by the end of January of the relevant calendar year.
Notifications shall be submitted electronically by a Data Box in PDF format.
The transport of raw tobacco must be accompanied by a document with the required formalities.
Excise tax legislation in SR
The legal framework governing the area of consumption taxes in SLOVAKIA comes from EU legislation, and thus helps create a uniform tax system.
Individual types of excise taxes are determined by the legislation of the SR, which is similar to the legislation of surrounding countries.
Definition of legislation in the SR
The legislative regulation of excise duties is provided by four laws according to individual subjects of taxation.
Harmonisation was achieved through the adoption of the following excise tax laws: act no 98/2004 Z. z., on excise duty on mineral oils, law no 106/2004 Z. z., on excise duty on tobacco products, law no 530/2011 Z. z., on excise duty on alcoholic beverages, law no 609/2007 Z. z., on excise duty on electricity, coal and natural gas.
All excise laws are the regulations of substantive law and deal with the taxation of the object of excise duties in the tax territory.
Law no 563/2009 Z. z. tax administration (tax code) is the precept of procedural law, governs the administration of taxes, the rights and obligations of taxpayers and other persons.
This legal framework transposed the various provisions of Council Directive 2008/118/EC of 16. December 2008 concerning the general arrangements for excise duty and repealing directive 92/12/EEC, and transposed the provisions of other directives and legislation of the European community.
Structure of amendments to the legislation for individual types of excise duties in relation to the subject of control in the SR
Since 2011, passed legislation relating to the management of excise taxes several fundamental changes according to the structure of excise taxes.
In the EMCS system was the monitoring of the transport of selected products subject to excise duties in the regime of conditional exemption from the tax changed from the paper of the accompanying administrative document to a solely electronic system, where are these transport tracked in real-time.
Under the EMCS electronic system, a suspension of access to the EMCS was introduced in 2015.
THISsegmentISintentionallyLEFTblank
The customs office has the possibility to suspend the access right in justified fear of an unpaid or undetermined tax from previous tax period and its unenforceability.
This applies to the maturity of the tax, since the excise goods are required for the composition of collateral, which, however, is released by the termination of transport.
Excise duty on mineral oils
A major change in the administration of the excise duty on mineral oils occurred in 2011, when the possibility of using so-called red diesel was abolished.
The marked gas oil, also commonly called red diesel, was among the mineral oils.
In the past red diesel used on specific statutorily defined purposes, e.g. in agriculture, and its use was discounted at a lower rate of excise duty.
This change had a positive impact on the revenue part of the state budget.
The aim of the abolition of red diesel was an effort to reduce the public deficit, simplify the system of taxation of mineral oils and reduce the administrative burden of the concerned business entities.
In 2012, a new type of tax entity was created, namely a fuel seller.
The purpose of this statutory change was to introduce a registration obligation for all service stations.
Clarification of the movement of taxed petrol and diesel is linked to the obligation to purchase petrol and diesel from a fuel distributor.
In 2014 there were introduced new concepts of tax entities, and distributor of fuel and the consumer of fuel.
That change contributed to the elimination of tax evasion on petrol and diesel and made the movement of these fuels clear (see Annex 4, diagram a).
As part of the fight against tax evasion, statutory provisions on the registration of tax entities trading in lubricating and base oils were extended.
However, in the SR, these mineral oils are not subject to the obligation of marking by an indicator.
Excise duty on tobacco products
In the framework of combating tax evasion and monitoring of tobacco raw material, the scope of the tobacco raw material Act was expanded and a new tax entity was introduced – the tobacco raw material trader.
Tobacco raw material is not a harmonised tobacco product and its movement is not monitored within the EU.
In addition, an obligation was introduced to register technological equipment for the production of tobacco products.
The legislation has brought a new system of ordering, assessing, printing, distribution, and use of control stamps intended for labeling of consumer packaging of tobacco products.
Cigarettes, cigars, cigarillos and tobacco are marked with a checkmark.
Under the new system the customer must check marks to request the customs office to issue control marks electronically, through the information system on collection of check marks.
This step introduced electronic communication between the tax entity and the tax administrator.
One state stamp printer was established-in the Kremnice Mint.
The exercise of tax oversight over the printing of stamps has also been introduced.
The changes contributed significantly to the elimination of tax evasion.
A new system of printing control marks strengthens the system of control of the goods, because of the control mark is generated, a unique identification number, through which it is possible to simply verify, whether the goods originated from legitimate sources.
Unique twelve-digit identification number (1.–2. the site forms a checksum; 3. the location determines whether the code belongs to the control mark or to a group of packages; 4. the site is a series identifier; 5.–8. the site is the alphanumeric part of the sequence; 9.–12. the place is the decimal part of the sequence) can also be applied in the form of a two-dimensional barcode.
The check mark intended for labeling of cigarettes shall be further listed the price of cigarettes, the sign for the validity of the rates of excise duty, number of pieces of cigarettes in the consumer package and length of cigarettes.
Excise duty on alcoholic beverages
The biggest legislative change has touched alcohol, wine and beer, because the original three rules of substantive law have been abolished and there was one common law on excise duty on alcoholic beverages.
The law was drafted, in particular because of the need of the general solution to the issue of the taxation of alcoholic beverages, the solution of their production, monitoring of movement, securing taxes, as well as the need to improve the business environment in the region, streamline the performance of the tax administration, reduce the administrative burden for small and medium-sized entrepreneurs.
A new way of addressing the issue of the taxation of individual types of alcoholic beverages has introduced the use of a single rate of excise tax on alcoholic beverage and to take into account the volumetric percentage of the actual alcohol content.
For non-sparkling wine, sparkling wine and fermented beverages is taken into account, the volumetric percentage of the actual alcohol content in the final product.
The concentration of beer is also expressed in the percentage by volume of the actual alcoholic strength of the finished product.
Was introduced the category of small producers of fermented beverages, whose essence lies in the exemption from excise tax for natural person, which makes a fizzy fermented beverage for their own consumption and for the consumption of his household not exceeding in amount 1 000 gallons for the marketing year.
The legislation brought a new system of ordering, assessing, printing, distribution and use of stamps intended for labelling consumer packages of alcohol.
Under the new system the customer must check marks to request the customs office to issue control marks electronically, through the information system on collection of check marks.
This step introduced electronic communication between the tax entity and the tax administrator.
One state stamp printer was established-in the Kremnice Mint.
The exercise of tax oversight over the printing of stamps has also been introduced.
The changes contributed significantly to the elimination of tax evasion (see Annex 4, diagram B) and the elimination of counterfeiting of control marks.
A new system of printing control marks strengthens the system of control of the goods, because of the control mark is generated, a unique identification number, through which it is possible to simply verify, whether the goods originated from legitimate sources.
Unique twelve-digit identification number (1.–2. the site forms a checksum; 3. the location determines whether the code belongs to the control mark or to a group of packages; 4. the site is a series identifier; 5.–8. the site is the alphanumeric part of the sequence; 9.–12. the place is the decimal part of the sequence) can also be applied in the form of a two-dimensional barcode.
Comparison and evaluation
Comparison
Excise taxes on alcohol, mineral oils, tobacco products, beer, wine and intermediate products in the CZECH republic are regulated by one common act no. 353/2003 Coll.
Fixed fuel tax, natural gas tax and some other gases and electricity tax are part of Act No. 261/2007 Coll.
In contrast, in the SR, each excise tax is governed by a special law, in addition to the law on excise duty on alcoholic beverages, which includes a tax on alcohol, beer, wine and intermediate products.
A special law regulates excise duty on electricity, coal and natural gas.
In the Czech Republic it is from 1. 1. 2015 issue of permits to dealing with products subject to excise duty according to the law on excise taxes, and conditional upon, inter alia by demonstrating the economic stability of the applicants by the customs authorities to annually verify the implementation of the financial analysis.
In SLOVAKIA a similar form of analysis realizes only when deciding to waive or reduce the tax.
OOTP SR shall exercise the tax supervision in the form of the presence of the employee of the financial directorate of the over use of control stamps for marking alcohol and tobacco products, their disposal in the printer and selling them to individual customers.
The law provides that the production of stamps is provided by the state enterprise Mint Kremnica.
The production of tobacco stickers and control tapes in the Czech Republic is not supervised by the customs authorities in the printer.
Tobacco stickers and the surveillance tapes taken from the printer entrusted with the local workplace customs office in Kutná Hora.
Tobacco stickers are taken over by their customers at this territorial workplace, and alcohol marking tapes are further distributed to individual local tax authorities according to the place of marking.
The legislation of the Czech Republic does not define the manufacturer of tobacco stickers and control belts.
In SR there is a duty of registration of technological equipment for the production of tobacco products or its parts, in the CZECH republic, such obligation is introduced.
In the Czech Republic tobacco sticker carries excise duty on tobacco products, which is paid when taking tobacco stickers at the designated customs office.
In SR, by contrast, there is no excise duty on tobacco products.
In the CZECH republic was in a controlled period introduced a refund of excise taxes on mineral oils in the case of their use for agricultural crop production, the so-called green diesel.
Since 2017, this tax refund has also been extended to livestock production.
In SR such support to farmers is not introduced (existed until 31. 12. 2010 as the so-called red diesel).
In order to strengthen the fight against tax fraud, a bail of 20 million was introduced in the Czech Republic for fuel distributors. CZK (i.e. € 740 thousand).
As a result of the introduction of this measure, the number of fuel distributors decreased from 1,891 entities in 2013 to 174 in 2014 (i.e. a decrease of 1,717 tax entities).
In SR, a similar Institute of a fuel distributor is introduced, but without the composition of the bail required to secure excise duty on mineral oils.
Sr registered 303 distributors in 2014 and 407 distributors in 2015.
In SR is introduced the institute of a retailer of fuel and consumer of fuel, which, permits are issued by the locally competent customs office.
There is no such Institute in the Czech Republic.
In the Czech Republic, selected mineral oils are labelled, and some other mineral oils are also labelled, in the SR after the abolition of the so-called red diesel, the marking of mineral oils is not applied.
In the CZECH republic the control tape for marking of alcohol contains eight-digit individual code that is used to verify the origin of ethyl alcohol and dvanáctimístný registration code with an indication of lihovitosti spirits, according to which a record is kept of the inspection belt.
Destruction, loss and return of the control tape are entered in the registry the following working day.
The holder of the tape is obliged to notify the use of the tape within the same period.
In the SR control mark used for marking of alcohol in consumer packaging contains unique language and identification number, which is in the case of its use once a month communicated to the tax authorities and used to verify the authenticity of the control signs.
The Register shall contain the number of inspection marks collected, used and claimed.
Both the Czech Republic and the Czech Republic have established the Institute of compulsory registration or registration of a distributor of alcohol.
In SR's registration be conditional upon compliance with the conditions of binding, inter alia, on the storage area exceeding 200 m2; the annual turnover from the sale of the consumer packaging of alcohol a minimum of 100 000 € or paid-up capital, at least in the amount of 100 000 €; minimum number of 10 employees.
In the Czech Republic, registration is subject, inter alia, to the deposit of CZK 5,000,000 (i.e. € 185,000) in favour of the tax administrator for the entire period of validity of the registration.

In the SR, in the production of alcohol not only in consumer packaging, the constant presence of the tax administrator is required.
In the CZECH republic is in the manufacture of ethyl alcohol in a consumer packaging required a special form of registration of persons required to mark the alcohol with a condition of bail in favour of the tax administrator in the amount of 100 000 Czk (i.e. 3 700 €) up to 5 000 000 Czk (i.e. 185 000 €) according to the quantity taken control of the tapes and the installation of tracking devices with constant access of the tax administrator.
Evaluation
The legislation of the CZECH republic and SLOVAKIA highly exceeds the minimum requirements of the EU on the subject, and the administration of excise duties and responds to identified risks from other member states as well as the risks identified in the tax territories.
Legislative changes adopted during the period under review allow tax authorities to prevent possible tax evasion more extensively.
In the Czech Republic and the Czech Republic in the fight against tax evasion in the form of misuse of tobacco raw materials (e.g. sheets), excise duty on raw tobacco or tobacco raw materials was introduced in addition to EU legislation.
Although the raw tobacco or tobacco material are not harmonised tobacco product, monitor the CR and SR of their movement.
The Czech Sao and Sao SR may recommend that that measure be applied in other EU member states.
In the CZECH republic good practice has shown that examining the economic stability of applicants for the issue of permits according to the law on excise taxes has proved successful, because it reduces the risk of tax arrears.
For this reason, both audit institutions recommend applying such checks also in SR conditions.
Distribution of control marks is in the SR more efficient than in the CZECH republic, because the burden of the customs authorities of the costs associated with transport between the printer and the customer control of the tapes and patches.
The financial administration of the SR has a better overview of the existence and location of technological equipment for the production of tobacco products.
However, in the Czech Republic it is more effective to collect tax on tobacco products, since the order of the tobacco sticker itself is a tax return with subsequent payment of tax.
The financial administration of SR has a better overview of the points of sale of propellants thanks to the introduction of the institutes "fuel seller" and "consumer of propellants".
The introduction of mandatory marking of mineral oils in the Czech Republic makes it easier to control the misuse of mineral oils at a reduced rate of tax or exempt.
In the CZECH republic (2013) and in SR (2014) introduced a new control tape, or mark containing the identification code.
The control tape in the Czech Republic also contains the registration code, while in the SR the new legislation has refrained from introducing it.
It is not yet possible to evaluate the effects due to the short effectiveness of legislative changes.
Introduction effective labeling of consumer packaging of alcohol control mark, or tape is an effective measure in the fight against tax evasion.
The SAO and the SAO of the Czech Republic may also recommend the introduction of this control measure in other member states.
The SR's attitude to the conditions for the distribution of alcohol characterizes the clientele approach, which does not block the funds of tax entities.
In contrast, the approach of the CZECH republic is rather restrictive, since it introduces a bail burdensome cash flow tax entities, but more reduces the risk of tax arrears.
Evolution of excise revenue
The excise tax is an indirect tax introduced by the state in order to increase the revenues of the state budget and also regulate the amount of sold goods, whose consumption is deemed harmful for the individual and/or company (regulatory function of taxes).
According to the commission communication: Europe 2020 – strategy for smart, sustainable and inclusive growth of 3. 3. 2010 under the flagship resource-intensive Europe initiative, the European Commission intends to improve the framework for the use of market-based instruments, including in the form of a revision of energy taxation with a focus on reducing energy and resource consumption.
To the fulfillment of the intent of the EC member states should endeavour, in the framework of a "greening" of tax systems to shift the tax burden from labour, inter alia, on energy and environmental taxation.
Collection of tax revenue from excise taxes in the CZECH republic and SLOVAKIA involves the collection of excise taxes on mineral oils, tobacco products, alcohol, beer, wine and intermediate products, on natural gas, solid fuels and electricity.
The share of excise taxes in total tax revenue and the share in GDP of monitors including the Organization for economic cooperation and development (OECD).
The two supreme audit institutions used the following selection criteria to enter a query on the OECD website.
Collection of excise duties in connection with macroeconomic indicators in the Czech Republic
In the Czech Republic, the share of excise taxes on total tax revenues and the share of GDP decreased slightly, according to OECD data.
For the conversion of amounts in CZK to € to 31. 12. the rate of the European Central Bank of the ECB was used for the year in question.
The nominal rate of CZK against € in 2013 decreased by 9.1% year-on-year against 2012 (from 25,140 to 27,425).
This was mainly due to the monetary policy decision of the CNB Banking Board of 7. November 20136.
The resulting values of collection of excise duties, rates of excise duties and income per capita in € decreased significantly due to the exchange rate difference.
A significant reduction in the share of excise taxes in 2014 was due to one-off shortfall of revenue from the excise tax on tobacco products due to the impact of new legislation restricting the sale of tobacco products with old tax rate.
The share of excise taxes is also influenced by the growth of the collection of taxes on income as a result of improved general economic situation of the Czech republic significantly increased.
The total collection of excise taxes has the largest share of excise tax on mineral oils (in 2015 approximately 55,7 %), the however, despite the significant growth of the economy against the year 2012 fell.
Collection of excise duty on mineral oils in 2013 and 2014 was significantly lower than in 2012 and 2015, although in 2013 as a measure against tax fraud introduced the registration of distributors of motor fuel.
The trend in eco-friendly vehicles and biofuel support is negatively reflected in the tax return.
A negligible proportion they have tax on gas, tax on solid fuels and tax on electricity, which in comparison with the surrounding states due to the low tax rate, which is close to the minimum rates set by the EU.
If there is no rate hike, will be in the future, their share with regard to the ever decreasing energy performance of buildings and manufacturing processes fall.
Collection of excise duty from ethyl alcohol in 2013 and 2014 was negatively affected by the aftermath of large-scale case of tax fraud relating to the marketing of tax-free ethyl alcohol, alcohol containing methanol or insufficiently denatured alcohol into the bloodstream in the form of spirits.
In 2015, following the adoption of a number of measures against such action and the recovery of the spirits market, the collection of excise duty on alcohol excised by £ 4m in 2012. €.
The share of the tax on tobacco products increased as a result of rising rates.
Basic rates of excise taxes between the years 2012-2015 change in the tax on tobacco products, where there was an increase in rates, in particular due to compliance with the Council directive 2011/64/EU on the structure and rates of excise duty on tobacco products.
Due to monetary intervention of ČNB, the real rate of excise duties in €, excluding the tax on tobacco products, decreased significantly. Tobacco products have risen only slightly.
In relation to the price growth, GDP or the level is not set indexation of rates of excise taxes, may not then be filled with the feature of excise taxes consisting in the regulation of socially problematic activities.
With the economic growth of the Czech Republic and the growth of living standards, real excise rates are reduced.

Administrative expenditure of excise duties
The effectiveness of administrative costs reflects the correlation between expenditure and revenue related to the administration of excise duties, i.e. expresses the amount of expenditure per 100 units of income (CZK, €).
The higher the resulting value, the worse the efficiency of administrative costs.
The efficiency of the tax administrator in the administration of tax affects the scope and organisational structure of the tax administrator, the management of the organization, the legal environment and the level of computerization of individual activities.
The determination of the effectiveness of the administrative costs of tax administration by the conversion rate method is based on the number of employees involved in excise management in the line-managed structure.
In the Czech Republic excise duty management is carried out in addition to other activities by the customs administration of the Czech Republic, which is a separate organizational component of the state and an entity.
In the Slovak republic tax administration provides Financial administration of the Slovak republic, with the authorities of the customs administration are the internal organizational unit, costs and returns are included collectively, for the entire organizational unit.
Therefore with regard to the possibility of comparing the efficiency of the administration of excise taxes in the calculation of the efficiency of the administrative costs included expenditure and revenue Financial administration of the CZECH republic.
Administrative costs of excise tax administration in the Czech Republic
Excise administration is a complex of administrative acts, which is carried out mainly by the customs administration of the Czech Republic.
Some partial control acts are carried out by other public authorities, but their importance is negligible.
In particular, excise management is carried out by the following departments:
Directorate-General Customs
Department 23 tax
department 231 – the Methodology of the tax monitors and proposes legislative measures, ensures the interpretation of laws, methodically directs and coordinates: the performance of the agendas of the administration of taxes and related legislation, especially tax management and related control and supervisory activity, the administration of the transport of selected products;
Department 232-ELO and search performs search and methodically manages traffic controls of selected products and ensures international cooperation between ELO and EMCS;
Department 233-tax inspections methodically manages and coordinates the implementation of the tax inspection agenda at customs offices;
department 30 legal
department 301 – Legal carries out methodology activities in the areas of administrative punishment, administrative procedure, the process of tax inspections, the registration procedure, nalézacího management, payment of taxes, fines for late claim taxes, penalty and interest;
department 302 – Administrative activities performs decision-making activities in cases where the legislation provides for the scope of the DGC, e.g. the decision about the delegation of territorial jurisdiction subject to another materially competent tax administrator, the decision on attraction, i.e. taking things to the supervisor by the tax administrator, an appeal against decisions of customs authorities and examine the incentives for inaction in the tax and administrative proceedings;
department 303 – of the revenue Administration and enforcement methodologically manages, coordinates and performs tasks in the framework of international cooperation in the recovery of tax arrears and implementation of tasks in the area of insolvency proceedings;
Department 60 analysis and information support
department 601 – Risk and criminal analysis, and ensures and performs risk analysis, and participates in the management of executive risk and the planning of control activities and control actions;
Department 604-Financial Analysis carries out financial analysis in the customs administration, in particular in the framework of the authorisation procedure.
The customs authorities carry out activities within the framework of the agenda in different locations of the region, and even the agendas are scattered in multiple locations:
department 02 – Analysis and information support, which performs risk analysis, managing risk profiles, and the collection and evaluation of information from all available sources of information;
Department 1 legal
department 11 – Legal and administrative activities, which handles the documentation, the opinion and the order for reference, reports for the appellate body, issues decisions on the authorisation in connection with the administration of excise duties and environmental taxes, the law on compulsory labelling of alcohol and the law about alcohol, decides in the matter of ensuring payment on yet nesplatnou or has not yet nestanovenou tax;
department 3-tax
department 31 – a Tax that carries on the agenda: the tax supervision on tax subjects, e.g. control of compliance with the conditions set in the issued permits, supervision over the functionality and accuracy of manufacturing equipment for the production of ethyl alcohol and determining the quantity and concentration of the produced ethyl alcohol, professional supervision in the denaturing of alcohol, physical control in the area of administration of excise taxes; non-tax controls in the area of inspections on the basis of laws with an indirect relationship to consumption taxes, in particular the control of the compulsory tagging and coloring selected mineral oils, the control of taxation of selected products, control the labelling of tobacco products, control, whether the seller or the buyer for violation of the law on prices and other price regulations, is carrying out acts in connection with the law on fuels, carried out acts in connection with the law on compulsory labelling of alcohol and the law about alcohol, carried out acts in connection with the fulfilment of the obligations minimum amount of biofuels into free tax circulation for transport purposes; the registration of economic agents to taxes, registering persons liable indicate alcohol and distributors of ethyl alcohol and the registration of distributors of motor fuel; tax administration, in particular, the leadership of the tax proceedings in the matter of assessment and prescribing, where appropriate, tax refund, monitoring of the provision of the tax and its use for the payment of taxes, the implementation of the search;
department 39 – Tobacco stickers, and the control strip – the organisational unit of the Customs office for Central bohemian region and carries out activities in the areas of ordering, production and distribution and disposal of tobacco stamps and of the control belt.
For the disposal of returned/damaged tobacco stickers, representatives of the customs office and representatives of the DGC are present, who supervise the liquidation process and write a record of the liquidation.

After the physical shredding of the control tapes has been carried out, the chairman of the liquidation Commission shall ensure that the data on the destroyed control tapes are recorded;
department 5-checks,
department 52 - tax inspections carry out tax inspections;
Department 6 – supervision

department 62-mobile supervision carries out the control of the transport of selected products on the way.

the department of excise duties – directs and coordinates activities in the field of the administration of excise taxes; drawing up expert opinions; making proposals and comments to legislative changes; makes decisions about the delegation of territorial jurisdiction to tax entities; allocates and deleted the registration sample numbers;

Department of Appeals for excise duties and customs duties):

Customs offices:
