stations of the customs office – the performance of tax supervision over the possession and movement of goods subject to excise duties; ensures performance of the permanent tax surveillance in a tax warehouse for alcohol; decide on security and on confiscation of goods.
SR financial management expenditure on excise duty management is constantly increasing as investment in efficient tax management and the electronisation of financial management, with the exception of wage growth, increases.
Although excise revenue grew, spending grew faster as a result of Unitas-related it adjustments.
Wage expenditure is significantly affected in the SR by the performance of permanent tax supervision in alcohol tax warehouses, which the Czech Republic does not apply.
Expenditures of the Customs administration of the CZECH republic on the administration of excise taxes between 2012 and 2015, significantly increased in 2015, this growth was mainly due to the growth of wage expenditure and expenditure on technical support.
In the Czech Republic, excise revenue grew at about the same rate.
Wage expenditure in the Czech Republic is positively influenced by the broader competences of the customs administration, e.g. weighing trucks, checking the performance of duties in connection with the myth.
The efficiency of administrative costs in SR shows a slightly worsening trend year on year.
The number of employees did not change significantly, but spending per employee grew.
The number of employees did not change significantly in the Czech Republic, but spending per employee grew more slowly compared to the Czech Republic.
Evaluation
In the Czech Republic and the Czech Republic, wage growth is an important factor in the impaired efficiency of administrative expenditure, which can be assessed as a natural development.
In both countries, maintaining considerable administrative difficulty in the management of excise duties appears to be a negative factor, which is confirmed by the reduced number of employees in the excise management sector.
In the SR, however, the administration of excise duties on lower incomes is significantly more demanding on personnel capacity.
Performance indicators of Excise Management
The administration of excise duties is a set of activities aimed at correctly identifying, determining and securing the payment of tax.
The main processes in the administration of excise taxes are tax assessment, permitting and registration activities, traffic surveillance, inspection and search of the tax bodies.
The number of administrative acts and managed entities is an indicator of the performance of the tax administrator.
The correlation between the reference indicator and the number of tax administrators expresses the effectiveness of the work of the tax administrator and defines the cost of particular activities.
Authorisation and registration activities are a fundamental prerequisite for dealing with selected products for business purposes and their transport in the regime of conditional exemption from tax.
The tax administrator is required in subjects with the permission of or registration to perform the continuous management with a focus on supervision on the implementation of legislation and the conditions laid down by the tax administrator, which must be allocated adequate personnel resources.
The endpoint was the number of authorisations or registrations in force at 31. Dec.
The number of authorisations or registrations issued is not identical to the number of tax entities.
Administrative acts are specific administrative acts in the case.
Pursued administrative acts are the frequency of the most significant acts of the tax administrator (tax assertion, the administration of transport in the EMCS), or activities that are a sequence of actions ending in the report or decision.
Performance indicators in the Czech Republic
Authorization and registration for activities in the Czech Republic
Tax warehouse:
To produce, process, store, send or receive the selected products can be based on authorization of the tax administrator to operate a tax warehouse.
If the tax warehouse operator has multiple warehouses, a permit is issued for each separately, including the provision of tax.
Ensure tax is not required in the case of distilleries under a permanent tax supervision of the tax administrator (i.e., the physical presence of official persons, and ensuring the equipment packages, the tax administrator).
In the Czech Republic, permanent tax oversight is not applied.
The tax warehouse operator is also registered for tax under Section 125 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.
Authorisation to operate a tax warehouse is a prerequisite for the transport of selected products exempt from tax from the place of importation to a tax warehouse, authorized recipient in another member state, to the point of export in another member state or a recipient in another member state (replaced by the status of authorised consignor as referred to in article. Article 4 (4) 10 council directive 2008/118 / EC).
Tax warehouse statistics do not include permits for the acquisition of electricity, natural gas and solid fuels, excluding tax, which are analogues of the tax warehouse permit.
Cultivation Brandy produces alcohol with a reduced 50% tax rate (14 300 CZK/hl of ethanol) – fruit spirits for growers. It is not a tax warehouse, and the permit for operation is issued by the Ministry of Agriculture.
A reduced rate of tax can be applied to 30 liters of pure alcohol per household grower intended for personal consumption for the production period (July–June).
Evidence of the burning, which lead operators of distilleries, and made available to the tax authorities, must contain information about the growers, the basic raw material, issued by the distillate, the origin of the fruit and the production of distillate.
The authorized recipient for repeated receiving the selected products and the authorized recipient for one-time adoption of selected products is on the basis of the authorization of the tax administrator and the specified conditions is entitled to a lump sum to accept or repeatedly receive selected products under the suspension system transported from another member state.
The beneficiary is not the operator of the tax warehouse and may not store or dispatch the selected products under the conditional exemption scheme.
User-selected products exempt from tax is a legal or natural person that receives and uses, where applicable, pursuant to section 52a or section 53 of act no. 353/2003 Coll. sells to the next user selected tax-exempt products; users have the status of tax entities without the obligation to register for tax.
To receive and use selected products exempt from tax can be only on the basis of a final permit, and only from the supplier referred to in the permit.
On the basis of an authorisation, exempt mineral oils may be sold to another holder of a licence for use or to a user who is authorised to use mineral oils without authorisation.
Without permission, mineral oils exempt from tax can be sold in legally established cases, for example.:
waste oil in quantities of less than 10 000 litres per calendar year, if the user himself made or incurred in its activities,
exempt selected mineral oils in unit packages of a capacity not exceeding 20 litres intended for purposes other than motor propulsion or heat production and intended for sale to the final consumer at the same time.
Exempt goods may be transported with proof of exemption.
After compulsory registration with the tax administrator, the alcohol Distributor in the consumer package is entitled to sell or otherwise transfer the alcohol entered for free tax circulation.
The storekeeper for raw tobacco is based on registration with the tax administrator and the specified conditions is entitled to store raw tobacco for any purpose other than for the manufacture of tobacco products.
A person dealing with special mineral oils is on the basis of registration with the tax administrator and the specified conditions be entitled to acquire, sell or otherwise transfer the special mineral oil that are freely delivered or placed in packaging exceeding 220 litres.
Distributor of fuel is on the basis of issued concessions and the registration of the tax administrator under the specified conditions is entitled to sell fuel on the territory of the Czech republic, with the exception of sales of fuel from the gas station.
PHM transport shall be accompanied by a tax document, a sales document or a transport document, as appropriate, a delivery plan and bottling tickets.
Such documents may be replaced by electronic documents sent before the commencement of transport to the tax authority.
The operator of the gas station is the owner of fuel sold at the gas station.
Gas stations are places where, under the permission of the Construction Authority, the sale or dispensing of PHM is allowed, as a rule, to the fuel tank.
The ministry of industry and trade of the records of the pumping stations and their operators, broken down by: registered – the current sale or dispensing of FUEL as a rule, into the fuel tanks of vehicles; with the defined access – operation as a rule in different business areas (e.g., quarries, sawmills, agricultural farms, transport organisations, building yards), the sale takes place there for the other side, limited on the basis of specific contractual relations; non-public – dispensing points, fuel only for own consumption of the operators.
The gas station is not a building or facility in the form of operational tanks placed in operation (e.g. on the chassis), if the fuel be issued only for your own use.
Operating tanks are not subject to the authorization of the tax administrator and are not registered.
Natural and legal persons may purchase, receive and sell liquefied petroleum gases put into free tax circulation for resale under the authorisation of the tax administrator.
They must also be authorised when they purchase or obtain liquefied petroleum gases for their own consumption exceeding 20 tonnes per calendar year.
Administrative operations in the Czech Republic
Tax control is a set of acts. The subject of tax inspections, tax obligation, the claim of the tax body or other circumstances decisive for the proper findings and determination of tax relating to one tax management.
Tax control can be carried out jointly for multiple tax procedures of one tax entity.
Repeated tax control can be carried out only under the statutory conditions and justification when the inspection is initiated.
Tax inspection is carried out within the time limit for tax assessment, which shall be three years, whereby the period for the conditions set by law, shall be extended by one year (e.g., administration of the additional tax proceedings, initiation of criminal proceedings in connection with such taxes), or puts (proceedings, international cooperation).
The deadline for fixing the tax shall expire no later than ten years after the deadline for filing a proper tax claim.
The tax administrator is not required to carry out a tax inspection for each tax entity.
The initiation of the tax audit puts the deadline for the possibility of filing an additional tax return or additional billing tax entity (§ 141 of the act no. 280/2009 Coll.) and reopens the deadline for setting the Tax (Section 148 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.).
On the basis of its result, an ex officio tax may be obtained.
The local ip is the individual time-bounded action (one day), in which the tax administrator finds evidence and carried out inspection of premises, goods, documents, records, means of transport and transport packaging, with the tax bodies and other persons participating at the tax administration at the location outside the premises of the tax administrator (e.g. with the tax body at the point of sale, on the way in transport).
The tax administrator is entitled to borrow documents and things, take samples or, if necessary, arrange them.
Based on the outcome of a local investigation cannot independently assess the tax tax, but can tax entity may invite to submit an amended tax return (§ 145 para. 2 of Act No. 280/2009 Coll.).
Checking traffic data in the EMCS system is not a local investigation.
The order of control tapes for marking of alcohol can tax the locally relevant point of marking make only a registered person liable to mark the alcohol and is carried out through the intelligent forms, which are automatically imported into the app registry značitelů alcohol.
The tax administrator processes the order, evaluates the adequacy of the ordered amount of control tapes and orders production.
He does not supervise the production of control tapes.
Production is provided by the state printer cenin, a state enterprise.
The customer of the control tapes takes over the control tapes at the tax administrator of the local place of marking.
Order tobacco stamps for marking of cigarettes, cigarillos, cigars and smoking tobacco performs the function of a tax return.
The value of the tobacco labels corresponds to the amount of tax liability, and the buyer of tobacco stamps is obliged to pay their value within 60 days from the date of their removal from the tax administrator.
The customer is obliged to calculate in the order itself the value corresponding to the amount of tax liability of the ordered tobacco stickers.
This period shall apply only if the value of the tobacco stickers is assured.
Order tobacco stamps shall be made on a form provided by the Ministry of finance in writing or through a data box with the possibility of use of intelligent forms.
The production of tobacco stickers is provided by the state printer cenin, a state enterprise.
Authorized by the tax administrator, which is the Customs office for Central bohemian region (territorial workplace Kutná Hora), ensures the purchase and transport of tobacco stamps to the tax authorities, which is further distributed and further examine their transport, storage and use in purchasers.
Tax claims include proper tax returns, supplementary and corrective tax return, including orders of tobacco stamps, administered by the tax bodies.
Included is not an admission of tax under the customs procedure on the basis of customs declarations and returns claims for refund of: mineral oils used for heat production, other gasoline used in the context of business activities otherwise than for the production of heat or drive engines, mineral oils used for agricultural primary production.
The fines imposed include an administrative procedure for dealing with the infringements identified, which is a set of follow-up administrative acts. International exchange of information on tax entities (ELO) within the meaning of Council regulation (EU) no 389/2012 currently underway in the form of: request on administrative cooperation, response to a request for administrative cooperation, spontaneous information, news about events, messages about control.
Transport occurring in the regime of conditional exemption from tax between the Czech republic and the EU member states – the Czech customs office is the tax administrator of the receiving or the sending tax warehouse or authorized recipient.
Performance indicators in SR
Authorisation and registration for activities in SR
The administration of excise taxes in the SR provide mainly the customs authorities and the department of excise section of the customs and tax OOTP SR, whose procedure in the administration of excise taxes govern the individual laws on excise taxes and the tax code.
These laws determine not only the scope of authorizations for the CÚ and FŘ SR in the administration of excise duties, but also the rights and obligations of tax entities in connection with registration or payment of excise duty.
The largest year-on-year increase in tax bodies (about 234 %) was recorded in 2012 and 2013, which was due to the increase in permits issued within the tax warehouses, the increase in the registration of the authorized recipient for repeated receiving and registering of a large number of user enterprises.
The legislation clarified the transport of some bulk mineral oils, as well as the notification obligation, if they are transported loosely or in containers of a capacity exceeding 150 litres or 230 liters, and also expanded the list of mineral oils which are subject to the control and procedure during the transport of other goods, such as medicines against the knocking of the engines, oxidation inhibitors, živicové inhibitors, agents for improving the viscosity, anti-corrosive preparations.
For lubricating oils, a mandatory indication was introduced concerning the indication of their kinematic viscosity.
Approach the registration process for the selected tax entities within the meaning of national legislation in the SR is specified in the following sections of the document.
Tax warehouse operator
In the framework of the national legislation of the SR during the registration the operator of a tax warehouse in all the subjects of excise taxes the person who wants to operate a tax warehouse must ask at the same time also on the registration and issuance of a permit to operate a tax warehouse.
The final decision in the registration process is the registration certificate for the relevant excise duty, which the operator of the tax warehouse acquires legal status for all tax warehouses.
At the same time the CA issue the authorisation to operate a tax warehouse, which authorizes the operator of a tax warehouse in the said tax warehouse produce, process, store, receive or dispatch of the selected products in the regime of conditional exemption from tax.
In the event that the operator of a tax warehouse tax warehouses in multiple locations, the tax administrator shall issue to each tax warehouse, a separate authorisation to operate a tax warehouse.
The transport of the object of excise duty under the conditional exemption scheme is monitored electronically through the EMCS system.
For each transport, a unique reference code is generated, the so-called.
Arc code under which the said transport can be monitored online and thus in real time.
If the operator of the tax warehouse at the same time, a person authorised for distribution of ethyl alcohol, is obliged to notify electronically the CA business name of the consumer packaging of alcohol, the volume and the volumetric concentration of ethyl alcohol in consumer packaging of alcohol and the bar code of the EAN for each new kind of consumer packaging, which lists the into free tax circulation, and no later than the day of its launch.
Registered sender
A registered shipper is a special type of tax entity, which cannot be simultaneously registered also as the operator of a tax warehouse, even when sent subject to the excise tax in the regime of conditional exemption from the tax after its release for free circulation.
Under the national legislation of the SR, when registering a registered consignor in the framework of all excise items, a person wishing to send the excise subject under the conditional exemption procedure after his release into the customs procedure "free circulation" must also apply to the CÚ at the same time to register and issue permission to send the excise subject under that procedure.
The CÚ shall issue a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty and at the same time issue an authorisation to dispatch the object of excise duty under the conditional exemption procedure after its entry into the customs procedure "free circulation".
Cultivation Brandy
The basic function for the operation of the cultivation burn is to obtain a permit for the production of alcohol at the distillery plant from the Ministry of Agriculture and Rural Development Sr.
However, the permit itself from the ministry does not authorize the holder of the permit to operate the cultivation burn.
In order for a person to operate a cultivation burn, he / she must submit an application for registration and the issue of a certificate of registration of the cultivation burn operator.
The CÚ shall issue a certificate of registration for the relevant excise duty, which at the same time entitles the operator of the cultivation spirit to produce alcohol in the cultivation spirit.
The purpose of cultivation moisture is to provide services to growers.
Cultivation moonshine can not be a tax warehouse.
The legislator makes it possible to apply a reduced tax rate of 50% of the basic rate of tax, i.e. €540/hl A.
The reduced rate of tax shall be applied to alcohol produced in the cultivation burn for a quantity not exceeding 43 litres. per grower and his household for one production period in tax territory.
The production period lasts from 1. 7. current year to 30. 6. the following year.
The production period is not identical with the calendar year, and therefore, it is possible within one calendar year, apply to made alcohol more than once a reduced rate of tax, because the alcohol produced in two production periods.
This is the production of alcohol outside the conditional exemption regime, which in practice means that the produced alcohol is in free tax circulation.
The grower pays not only excise duty and value added tax for the produced alcohol, but also the price for the services rendered.
Grower distilleries exposes growers vyskladňovací sheet, which serves not only as a document to prove the origin and manner of acquisition of alcohol, but also about the payment of excise taxes.
The transport of alcohol produced in this way shall not be subject to monitoring by the tax administrator.
Importer of consumer packaging
The national legislation allows persons who intend to within the business to import consumer packaging of spirits or cigarettes from the territory of a third state and placing him into free tax circulation in the tax territory, to request the CA for inclusion in the register of importers of consumer packaging.
The importer of the consumer packaging shall not register for the relevant excise duty but shall issue a certificate of inclusion in the Register of importers of the consumer packaging.
That certificate entitles the importer to import consumer packages of alcohol or consumer packages of cigarettes from the territory of a third state.
At the same time, it must lodge a tax guarantee in respect of the amount of alcohol or cigarettes it intends to put into free circulation before issuing the inspection marks.
The importer of the consumer packaging must be put into free tax circulation only consumer packaging marked with control mark.
For this reason, must submit to the customs office of export number and the identification number of the control stamps exported to the territory of a third state.
On importation, the importer is obliged to have the number of inspection marks imported back from the territory of a third state confirmed by the customs office of importation.
While imports of consumer packaging importer progresses within the meaning of the customs legislation, where the customs debt is the amount of the excise tax.
In the event that the consumer package is released for free circulation, the compound tax guarantee shall be returned to the importer or may be used to pay the customs debt.
The importer of consumer packaging is not a tax warehouse.
If the importer of the consumer packaging of spirits will at the same time, a person authorised for distribution of ethyl alcohol, is obliged to notify electronically the CA business name of the consumer packaging of alcohol, the volume and the volumetric concentration of ethyl alcohol in consumer packaging of alcohol and the bar code of the EAN for each new kind of consumer packaging, which lists the into free tax circulation, and no later than the day of its launch.
Seller of consumer packaging alcohol in free tax circulation
In order to monitor the movement of alcohol in free tax circulation and eliminate tax evasion, the legislator introduced a new Tax Institute of the retailer of consumer packaging of alcohol.
A person who wants to be the holder of the authorization for the sale, you must ask the CA about issuance of the permit and to meet the legal requirements (business license for business activities; integrity in relation to the intentional economic crimes; it wasn't for her after a period of ten years withdrawn permission to sell; is not in liquidation nor in bankruptcy).
Since it is a consumer package of alcohol in free tax circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting these goods.
For example, an invoice containing also the holder's distribution authorisation number is sufficient to demonstrate how the consumer packages acquire alcohol.
The holder of the permit is required for each place of business lead for the calendar month records of the number of received pieces of consumer packaging of alcohol, the number of issued units of consumer packaging of alcohol, the state of the stocks of ethyl alcohol in consumer packaging of alcohol to the last day of the month and recording of shortages or excess in the number received and issued consumer packaging of alcohol.
The holder of the authorisation shall be obliged to purchase or otherwise withdraw alcohol in consumer packages only from the person authorised to distribute it in the course of business.
Distributor of consumer packaging alcohol
In order to monitor the movement of alcohol in free tax circulation and eliminate tax evasion, the legislator introduced a new Tax Institute distributor of consumer packaging of alcohol.
A person intending to hold a distribution permit must apply to the CÚ for the issue of a distribution authorisation.
The applicant must meet the statutory conditions (the business license for the commercial trade; storage area exceeds 200 m2; the annual turnover from the sale of the consumer packaging of alcohol a minimum of 100 000 € or paid-up capital, at least in the amount of 100 000 €; minimum number of 10 employees; it has no arrears against the customs office; has no arrears on compulsory contributions; integrity in relation to the intentional economic crimes; he was for ten years withdrawn permission to sell; is not in liquidation nor in bankruptcy).
Since it is a consumer package of alcohol in free tax circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting these goods.
For example, an invoice containing also the holder's distribution authorisation number is sufficient to demonstrate how the consumer packages acquire alcohol.
The holder of the authorisation for distribution is required for each place of business lead for the calendar month records of the number of received pieces of consumer packaging of alcohol, the number of issued units of consumer packaging of alcohol, the state of the stocks of ethyl alcohol in consumer packaging of alcohol to the last day of the month and recording of shortages or excess in the number received and issued consumer packaging of alcohol.
The holder of the distribution authorisation shall be obliged to purchase alcohol in consumer packaging only from another person authorised to distribute it.
The person authorised to distribute shall notify the data for each calendar month by electronic means, up to 25. on the following calendar month.
Fuel dealer
Due to the monitoring of fuel in free tax circulation, as well as the elimination of tax evasion has introduced a new type of tax entity and the seller of the fuel.
On the territory of the SR there is no special regulation regulating gas stations.
That is why the petrol stations in the national legislation SR are incorporated as fuel sellers.
A person who wants to in the context of business activities in the tax territory to sell in free tax circulation petrol, diesel or LPG for final consumption, is required before the sale ask the CA to issue a permit for the sale and submit a document proving that the storage device is certified and equipped with the appropriate certified test equipment capable of when income and expenditure to measure the amount of mineral oil, and the tank must be in accordance with the technical standards.
If the seller is a fuel, the operator of the tax warehouse, an authorised consignee or registered consignor, the CA issued automatically to registered persons also have permission to sell fuel.
The seller of fuel is required in addition to other statutory obligations to keep records of purchased and sold gasoline, diesel fuel or LPG for the calendar month and also is obliged to notify the CA of a new supplier (distributor) of fuel.
The seller of propellants is legally obliged to purchase or otherwise withdraw propellants only from the distributor of propellants or from a registered person.
Since these are propellants in free tax circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting these goods.
However, when the supply of fuel via tank truck prints the distributor during the pumping of fuel by sellers of the so-called stáčenku of a measuring device built in autocisterně.
That document shall also contain, in addition to the quantity data, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car allocated by the Traffic Inspectorate.
For example, an invoice containing also the number of the fuel distributor allocated by the Tax Administrator shall be sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of propellants.
The tax administrator in the territory of the SR in the exercise of tax supervision over mineral oils records tax evasion related to the transportation of this type of goods.
Primarily it is about trying to avoid in the transport of road checks, therefore, the carriers use the side roads, bypassing the system of toll collection because of the difficult monitoring of actual shipments.
Mineral oil transports are also carried out in converted double-bottomed tanks.
Many times it happens that the illegal transport of accompanying the vehicle, which carriers report possible mobile patrols in order to change the route and avoid the road check.
There is also a mixture of propellants with light fuel oils or waste oils.
Propellant Distributor
Due to the monitoring of fuel in free tax circulation, as well as for the purpose of elimination of tax evasion has introduced a new type of tax entity, and distributor of fuel.
A person who intends to tax of the territory in the framework of the business activity to distribute in free tax circulation petrol, diesel or LPG, is required before distribution may ask the customs office for the issue of permits for distribution and submit a document proving that the storage device is certified and equipped with the appropriate certified test equipment, as well as the list of suppliers and customers.
Distributor of fuel is required in addition to other legal obligations maintained separately for each establishment a register of purchased and sold gasoline, diesel fuel or LPG for the calendar month.
The propellant Distributor is legally obliged to purchase or otherwise withdraw propellants only from the propellant distributor or from a registered person.
Distributor of fuel may sell to the tax territory only to the distributor of fuel, the registered person or a consumer fuel.
However, when the supply of fuel via tank truck distributor of prints when transfer of fuel, sellers of fuel or a consumer fuel, the so-called stáčenku of a measuring device built in autocisterně.
That document shall also contain, in addition to the quantity data, the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car allocated by the Traffic Inspectorate.
Since these are propellants in free tax circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting these goods.
For example, an invoice containing also the number of the propellant distributor or registered person assigned by the tax administrator is sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of propellants.
Consumer of propellants
A special position in the national legislation is occupied by the consumer of propellants.
The person on the tax territory of the purchases in free tax circulation to your own consumption of petrol, diesel or LPG and the mineral oil is stored in a storage device, the volume of which is 15 000 liters and more, is obliged to notify this fact to the customs office at the latest before the first placement in a storage facility.
The consumer of propellants shall be registered by the customs office.
The latter is obliged, in addition to legal facts, to indicate the address of the location of the storage facility.
In practice, these are large transport companies, cooperatives, bus companies, road construction companies and other entities.
Storage facilities must be verified and fitted with measuring equipment allowing in the income and expenditure to measure the amount of fuel (stavoznak, measurement rod).
The tank must meet technical standards.
The consumer of propellants must purchase propellants only from a propellant distributor or from a registered person.
Since these are propellants in free tax circulation, an accompanying document is not required when transporting.
However, when the supply of fuel via tank truck distributor of prints when transfer of fuel to the consumer the so-called stáčenku of a measuring device built in autocisterně.
That document contains not only data relating to the quantity, also the date and time of delivery and the registration number of the car assigned to the transport inspectorate.
For example, an invoice containing also the number of the fuel distributor allocated by the Tax Administrator shall be sufficient to demonstrate the method of acquisition of propellants.
The tax administrator in the territory of the SR in the exercise of tax supervision over mineral oils records tax evasion related to the transportation of this type of goods.
Small independent brewery
The operator of a small independent brewery is a person who, in the course of business manufactures beer and meets the legal requirements.
Provided that the conditions set by law, can a small independent brewery to apply a reduced rate of tax, i.e. 2,652 € per hl/percentage of the volume of actual alcohol content.
Annual beer production is limited to up to 200,000 hl of beer.
Since the production of beer is outside the conditional exemption regime, the transport does not require an accompanying document because it is in free tax circulation.
A small independent brewery can not be a tax warehouse.
In practice, these are small family businesses, which also operate restaurants or taps in which they offer their own beer for sale.
Administrative operations in SR
This sub-chapter approximates the exercise of tax oversight of excise administration for selected tax entities within the meaning of national legislation in the Sr.
The largest annual increase in administrative operations (by 5.3 %) was recorded between 2012 and 2013, which was due to the implementation of more traffic in the EMCS system.
In contrast, the biggest decline was recorded year-on-year in 2014, up 4.3%, due to fewer tax checks completed and fewer tax returns filed.
The decline concerned legislative changes.
Tax controls
By exercising a tax control, the CÚ identifies or examines the facts decisive for the correct determination of the tax.
The staff of the CA in the exercise of tax control to demonstrate a mandate for the performance of a tax audit, which contains, inter alia, the purpose and the subject of control and the scope of the audited tax period.
In practice, this means that the Controlled tax period can be one month, but also more tax periods.
The scope of the Controlled tax periods is determined by the CÚ.
The tax inspection begins with the registration of the start of the tax inspection.
The Cú will confirm the receipt of the documents.
Borrowed documents the CÚ is obliged to return within 30 days from the end of the tax inspection.
The CÚ employee shall draw up a protocol from the tax inspection.
If the tax inspection finds out the difference in the sum, which was controlled by the tax body to pay, declare, or on which the claim for refund, send the CA together with the protocol, the inspected taxpayer concerned also a challenge to express to the findings set out in the protocol.
The tax inspection is completed on the day of delivery of the protocol.
The time limit for carrying out the tax inspection shall be not more than one year from the date of its initiation.
Tax inspection the registered persons and the selected registered persons shall be carried out as necessary, but at least once the day of termination of the right to establish the tax, which is 5 years.
FD SR issued an internal management act adjusting the above deadlines due to the uniform procedure of the tax administrator in the territory of the SR.
Local inquiries
The local investigation is an activity, the tax administrator, within which searches for evidence, examines and investigates the facts, which are necessary for the purposes of tax administration.
The CÚ staff member shall write a record of the local investigation and submit a copy of it to the tax entity.
When conducting a local investigation, the CÚ employee has the right to unrestricted access to land, operational buildings, rooms and places, including means of transport, transport packaging and accounting documents.
The clearing of the quantities of alcohol produced shall be carried out in the form of a local investigation.
The facts identified are the basis for the exercise of tax control.
In carrying out a local investigation, the CÚ is also entitled to take samples as well as to secure the matter.
FD SR issued an internal Management Act Regulating the exercise of Tax Oversight and local inquiries for individual subjects of excise duties in order to unify the procedures of the tax administrator.
Permanent tax oversight in alcohol tax warehouses
The entry of the Slovak Republic into the European Union on 1. 5. 2004 there was also a change in excise management.
The need for a more efficient spending of state budget funds in the administration of excise duty from ethyl alcohol, the improvement of the business environment in the region and the introduction of the legislative instruments for more effective suppression of grey economy in the area has resulted in in 2004, the adoption of new laws in connection with the administration of excise taxes.
One of the measures brought about by the new legislative change, was not only the transition of the tax administrator in the administration of excise duties from the tax authorities to the customs authorities, but also the introduction of the necessary presence of the tax administrator in the tax warehouse for alcohol.
On the territory of the SR national legislation determinatively defines that to accept, issue, produce or process alcohol in a tax warehouse is possible only in the presence of a CÚ employee.
This does not apply to a tax warehouse which accepts, stores or dispatches alcohol only in consumer packages.
At the same time, the CÚ has an obligation to ensure that employees in the tax warehouse are not limited to the income, supply, production or processing of alcohol.
The tax warehouse operator shall be obliged to ensure the working environment conditions for CÚ employees.
On the basis of a contract concluded with the FDC, the CÚ pays the cost of the lease to the tax warehouse operator on a monthly basis for the premises provided.
In a tax warehouse in the manufacture, processing or storage of alcohol shall be production facilities for the storage of ethyl alcohol adapted so that it was possible to determine at any time the amount of produced ethyl alcohol, processed ethyl alcohol, storage of ethyl alcohol including the stocks of ethyl alcohol and alcohol contained therein.
THISsegmentISintentionallyLEFTblank
Where alcohol is not accepted, dispensed, produced or processed in a tax warehouse, the customs office may waive the obligation to ensure the presence of a customs office employee and shall be obliged to secure the premises by closing the customs office.
In practice, however, this option too often not used because the operators of tax warehouses using continuous presence of an employee of the customs office in your favor.
Some tax warehouse operators use the legal option within the meaning of law no 467/2002 Z. z. on the production and marketing of ethyl alcohol on the market, and used production equipment for the production of ethyl alcohol in the distillery for the production burning and also for the purposes of the distillery on the spirits, which must be a tax warehouse.
About 250 customs officers are responsible for continuing tax oversight at alcohol warehouses.
Issuing of vouchers for the collection of alcohol stamps
The basic act for the collection of stamps is to send an application to the customs office for the allocation of a registration number and the issue of a voucher for the collection of stamps for alcohol.
Alcoholic beverage, which is alcohol, means goods of the combined nomenclature 2207 and 2208 with an actual alcoholic strength exceeding 1,2% by volume.
The control mark is intended for the labelling of consumer packages of alcohol.
Consumer packages of alcohol shall be considered as sealed consumer packages filled with alcohol intended for direct human consumption.
Consumer packaging combined nomenclature code 2207 and 2208 may be put into free tax circulation in the tax territory only if it is marked with a check mark.
Refer to the consumer packaging of alcohol control mark can only operator of the tax warehouse, authorized recipient and importer of the consumer packaging, which it will be put into free tax circulation.
The control mark shall contain, inter alia, an identification number consisting of a 14-digit numerical character. The identification number contains the registration sampling number (1.–6. instead of a numerical character), the volume of alcohol (7.–11. instead of numerical character) and the volume concentration of alcohol in the consumer package (12.–14. instead of a numerical character).
Original model of the alcohol inspection mark:
The registration sampling number shall be assigned by the CÚ to each customer separately.
The designation of the consumer packaging of alcohol may be used only the control mark, whose identification number corresponds to the volume of consumer packaging, the volume concentration of ethyl alcohol in consumer packaging and odběratelově control mark.
The national legislation at the end of 2014 brought about the introduction of a new information system of stamps.
The aim of the new information system of control marks was to simplify and informatizovat ordering system, assessing, printing, distribution, and use of control stamps designated for marking of the consumer packing of ethyl alcohol.
Refer to the consumer packaging of alcohol control mark can only operator of the tax warehouse, an authorised consignee, the importer of consumer packaging and the recipient (subscriber) of ethyl alcohol.
The buyer of the Stamps wishing to collect the stamps under the "new system" must request the customs office to issue the Stamps electronically.
Through the electronic system is a subscriber of the control marks required to apply for their release, to notify the data resulting from the national legislation of the SR and maintain a register of control marks.
The number of items of inspection marks ordered shall not be less than 500 or more.
Also, the tax administrator communicates with the customer control signs through the electronic system of control marks, and especially when reporting the number of control marks, which the customer may check marks to remove, or in determining the date of takeover of control marks customer of check marks in the printer.
The subscriber control signs is required before acceptance of the check marks to pass on account of the tax administrator the funds corresponding to the price control marks, which can remove and the quantity of which he shall notify to the customs office.
The price of the inspection mark shall take into account the amount of the printer's refund. However, it does not take into account the amount of excise duty.
Inspection marks is authorized to print the state enterprise Mint Kremnice.
FD SR exercises tax oversight over the handling and disposal of inspection marks in the printer.
FD SR is obliged to ensure the presence of a financial Directorate employee in the printer when handling inspection marks.
FD SR ensures the sale of the stamps to the customer of the Stamps in the printer.
It is possible to remove the Stamps only in the printer from an employee of the financial Directorate.
Issuing of vouchers for the collection of control marks on tobacco products
The customer of the control Mark must request the CU to allocate a registration sampling number and issue a voucher for the collection of the control mark.
The consumer packaging of cigarettes can only be put into free tax circulation when it is marked with a control mark.
Marking consumer packing of cigarettes control sign is possible only in the company, which manufactures cigarettes.
Purchaser of control stamps may be just the operator of a tax warehouse, authorized recipient or importer of tobacco products, who wants to indicate the tobacco products into free tax circulation in the tax territory.
Only a control mark may be used to indicate the consumer packaging of cigarettes, the number of cigarettes per pack, the length of cigarettes, the validity of the tax rate and the registration sampling number.
Consumer packaging of cigarettes can be sold for final consumption only at the price indicated on the control mark.
The national legislation at the end of 2014 brought about the introduction of a new information system of stamps.
The aim of the new information system of control marks was to simplify and informatizovat ordering system, assessing, printing, distribution, and use of control stamps designated for marking of the consumer packaging of tobacco, cigars, cigarillos, and cigarettes.
The buyer of the Stamps wishing to collect the stamps under the "new system" must request the customs office to issue the Stamps electronically.
Through the electronic system is a subscriber of the control marks required to apply for their release, to notify the data resulting from the national legislation of the SR and maintain a register of control marks.
Inspection marks is authorized to print the state enterprise Mint Kremnice.
FD SR exercises tax oversight over the handling and disposal of inspection marks in the printer.
FD SR is obliged to ensure the presence of a financial Directorate employee in the printer when handling inspection marks.
FD SR ensures the sale of the stamps to the customer of the Stamps in the printer.
It is possible to remove the Stamps only in the printer from an employee of the financial Directorate.
Refer to consumer packaging of tobacco control mark may an operator of a tax warehouse or importer of tobacco products.
Refer to the consumer packaging of cigars or cigarillos control mark may an operator of a tax warehouse, the importer of tobacco products or the legitimate beneficiary.
To mark the consumer packages of tobacco, cigars or cigarillos to apply only the control mark, whose data correspond to a character for the validity of the rates of excise duty.
It is only possible to mark the consumer packaging of cigarettes with a control mark in the company that produced them.
The number of items of inspection marks ordered shall not be less than 500 or more.
CA at the latest within three working days to electronically notify the purchaser of control stamps, the number of control marks, which can remove the price control mark and number of the account AND the SR.
The CÚ may reduce the number of items of inspection marks ordered if there are circumstances on the basis of which it can be reasonably assumed that there may be a breach of tax rules.
FD SR shall determine the date of receipt of the Stamps by the purchaser of the stamps, but not later than 10 days.
The date of acceptance of the stamps of the FD SR shall be notified by the buyer of the stamps via the electronic system of the Stamps.
Control marks issued by the financial directorate exclusively in the printer, but only after the receipt of the funds corresponding to their price on the account specified in the electronic notification of the customs office.
The subscriber control marks is required separately in the breakdown for cigarettes, cigars, cigarillos and tobacco keep a register of control marks in the electronic system of control marks.
Administrative cooperation between EU member states (ELO)
Within the meaning of Council regulation (EU) no 389/2012 department ELO and systems of the SPD of the department of excise AND SR is responsible for the security of information exchange on the basis of the application for administrative cooperation between the member states of the EU and the competent authorities of financial management.
These are, in particular, requests for vetting of excise management entities, requests for information relating to excise management, as well as requests for confirmation of information from the SEED database.
The exchange of applications shall take place in electronic form under the EMCS system.
The administrative cooperation between the member states of the EU are included the following acts: requests for administrative cooperation (a request for examination, request for information on the administration of excise taxes, a request for confirmation of the registration in the SEED); the response to the request of the administrative cooperation-spontaneous information; report on event; report of inspection.
Comparison and evaluation
Comparison
Authorisation and registration
In SR, the tax warehouse for alcohol is subject to permanent tax supervision, in the Czech Republic this supervision is replaced by continuous supervision of the tax administrator through a tracking device.
In the Czech Republic, small independent breweries are a tax warehouse, in the SR they are only registered by the tax administrator.
The Institute of registered consignor is established in the SR, which is included in the tax warehouses in the Czech Republic.
In SR it is possible to burn 43 litres of alcohol at a reduced rate of excise duty in case of cultivation burning.
In contrast, in the Czech Republic, the reduced alcohol tax rate can only be applied for 30 litres.
Cultivation fennel in SR must have permission not only from the Ministry of Agriculture and Rural Development SR, but also from the tax administrator.
In the Czech Republic, only the Ministry of Agriculture authorizes cultivation of moonshine.
In the SR, the import of consumer packages of alcohol is realized in addition to the operator of the tax warehouse also by the importer of consumer packages of alcohol.
The authorization of the importer is conditional on the registration of the applicant with the excise duty administrator.
In the Czech Republic, no special authorization of the tax administrator is required to import consumer packages of alcohol.
In SR, the sale of consumer packages of alcohol is conditional on the issuance of a permit of the tax administrator for the seller.
The retailer of consumer packages of alcohol has a statutory obligation to keep records of, inter alia, purchases and sales.
In the CZECH republic, the tax administrator no permission for the final seller for the consumer packaging of alcohol does not issue, it is sufficient to issue a concession for the sale of alcohol, the trade licensing office; the ultimate seller of any special register does not.
In sr the seller of propellants must have permission from the tax administrator to sell them.
National legislation in the SR does not provide any special regulation of the gas station, all the activities regarding gas stations are regulated only in the law on excise tax from mineral oils.
In the CZECH republic pumping station regulates the special act on fuels, the tax administrator, however, does not issue any permits to sell fuel.
Gas stations are registered and their list is published by the Ministry of industry and trade.
In SR, it is technically not possible to obtain a list of service stations from the financial management system.
In the SR there has been a significant increase in the number of selected permits or registrations of tax entities since 2012.
That increase was due to a legislative change in that period.
In the Czech Republic, on the contrary, the number of selected permits decreased significantly in 2013 due to the introduction of bail for fuel distributors.
Administrative acts
In the SR substantive legislation provides for the obligation to exercise tax control for selected tax entities.
This issue describes the internal control act, which issued the OOTP SR due to the application of a single procedure of tax administrators on the territory of the SR.
In the CZECH republic, the substantive laws of the obligation to the performance of tax audit provision, procedural regulation provides only for the possibility of inspection at the latest by the deadline for the tax assessment.
The reason for the large differences in the number of tax inspections and local investigations in the SR and CZECH republic is the fact that the internal control act of the OOTP SR provides, in what cases and in what time limits must of the tax administrator to perform tax inspection, while in the CZECH republic is the correctness of the declared amount of the excise or of the return to be verified in particular on the local investigation.
The number of comparable administrative operations in the Czech Republic has increased since 2012 due to an increase in traffic in the EMCS system and at the same time due to an increase in the number of tax returns filed.
In the SR had a number of administrative tasks between 2012 and 2015, a slightly increasing trend, which was affected by the increasing number of transport in the EMCS system and at the same time a decrease in the number of tax returns.
Evaluation
The large differences between the numbers of comparable authorisation and registration of tax subjects showed different legislation.
The number of comparable administrative acts of tax administrators was similar in the SR and the Czech Republic in each year of the period under review.
In the SR the total number of comparative tax subjects, which is about two thirds compared with the number of tax entities in the CZECH republic, accounting for approximately the same amount of administrative tasks.
From this it can be concluded that the SR is more focused on the implementation of administrative acts by the tax administrator, for example, the exercise of physical tax supervision.
In the Czech Republic, the emphasis is more on remote surveillance, such as tracking devices, imminent sending of data via the web interface and risk analysis.
Electronisation of Administrative Operations
Electronisation of administrative operations in the Czech Republic
The tax return can be filed through the Data Box.
The customs administration of the Czech Republic has introduced so-called interactive forms of tax returns, which, however, can no longer be processed automatically.
Further, the data must be rewritten into the personal tax account of the tax entity.
Benefit is the limitation of error filed tax returns (DAP), which set aside acts of the tax administrator relating to the management of corrections erroneously filed by the DAP.
DGC is working on a new DAP electronic processing app.
Through the intelligent forms can be further: given an application to the tax or registration to the activity and notification of changes to data, to assert claims for tax refund comply with the reporting obligations in the management of specific mineral oils, the handling of raw tobacco and the fulfilment of obligations in the field of biofuels.
Treatment with the control tapes is tax entities recorded in the information system ORO WebKlient, which is for registered entities available for registration with the tax administrator set of data.
Transport of selected products in the Czech republic in the regime of conditional exemption from the tax must be implemented in the CZECH republic on the basis of the electronic accompanying document, which is implemented in the CR as a national functionality to the electronic system for monitoring the transport of selected products (EMCS).
Transport of selected products in free tax circulation after the tax territory of the CZECH republic can be carried out always with the document evidencing their taxation, proof of exemption from excise duty, by decision of the customs office for the release of selected products into the customs regime, by a simplified accompanying document or any other decision on assessment of the excise tax.
The required content of data is determined by law.
Czech republic to facilitate the fulfillment of these obligations has introduced a voluntary electronic system for the issuing of alternative proofs (§ 5 and § 6 of act no. 353/2003 Coll.).
This allows the physical form of the documents to replace or supplement the electronically posted documents, which are through the web interface of the Customs administration of the CZECH republic sent to the data storage, where each such document is assigned a unique dvanáctimístný identification code (JIK).
JIK serves for the purpose of customs control on the way and makes it impossible to re-transport to the same document.
The largest operator of the tax warehouse of fuel in the CZECH republic, which states, roughly half the volume of PHM into free tax circulation, has a CS CR on-line access to the electronic filing system, to which the body automatically stores the issued tax documents.
EN the CZECH republic is considering the introduction of e-VDO, i.e. the electronic system for registration and monitoring of the transport of selected products carried out in free tax circulation.
This system should benefit from 70% of the existing EMCS functional specification.
The advantage will be a familiar environment for declarers and customs officers.
It will also be linked to the global guarantee system, the tax entities register or the risk analysis system.
The system should allow an overview of the dopravách in free circulation between the member states, which so far works on the basis of written documents without the recording and sharing of meeting numbers through simplified accompanying documents.
The risks of the current procedure of registration of transport of selected products in free tax circulation can be seen mainly in the abuse of the simplified accompanying document, repeated use of a single document or illegal materials without any document.
Electronisation of administrative operations in the SR
In the administration of excise taxation Financial management SR uses electronic communication in monitoring the movement of goods in the EMCS system in the regime of conditional exemption from tax, check marks, submission of tax returns and also in the registration and registration of tax entities.
In 2014 has also introduced a one-way electronic communication of tax bodies with the tax administrator, which was in 2016 extended to two-way communication.
In the context of electronic communication, the tax body after entering the access data zpřístupněnu a personal internet zone, the so-called electronic personal mailbox, which is intended for communication with the financial administration.
Within this zone has a tax entity access to the electronic registry through which the served application, notice, tax returns and other documents relating to the administration of excise taxes.
Electronic communication through the personal internet zone does not apply to all tax entities.
National legislation defines tax entities that are obliged to communicate with the tax administrator electronically.
These are mainly Value Added Tax Payers, tax advisors representing the tax entity and lawyers representing the tax entity.
The Sao SR also addressed the issue of the scope of the electronisation of Excise Management during the inspection.
These were only fully electronic acts, namely tax returns and electronic communications within ELO.
In the case of EMCs transport, there has been an increase in the electronisation of comparable administrative tasks selected, which is also a requirement for modern tax administration.

In the Czech Republic electronic processing of the tax return is not set.
In the Czech Republic, the possibility to insert mandatory documents for individual transport in free tax circulation is set up for tax entities on the website.
In the future, the announcement of transport in free tax circulation in the form and on the basis of the EMCS system is being prepared.

Reporting system of transport in free tax circulation in the CZECH republic contributes to the tax supervision, thereby eliminating the transport of selected products, where in conflict with the legislation had not been paid the excise tax.
Listed can be recommended as a good practice.

Organizational arrangement of Excise Management in SR
The Government of the Slovak Republic has set itself as one of the priorities of completing tax administration reform through the UNITAS programme, which will provide additional budgetary resources by combining tax collection, duties and levies and by suppressing tax evasion.
In this context, there has been the implementation of tax reforms at the central level, which brought about the merger of the Tax directorate of the SR and the Customs directorate of the SR into the Financial directorate of the SR and the emergence of financial administration.
FD SR was established on 1. 1. 2012 by law no 333/2011 Z. z. on bodies of state administration in the field of taxes, fees and customs, as amended, as a budgetary organisation, which has its registered office in Banska Bystrica and is connected to the state budget through the budgetary chapter of the Ministry of finance of the Slovak republic.
FD SR, CÚ and the Criminal Office of the financial administration within the meaning of law no 199/2004 Z. z. the Customs Act and amending and supplementing certain laws, as amended, are customs authorities, if they perform tasks according to customs regulations.
Within the meaning of law no 333/2011 Z. z. on bodies of state administration in the field of taxes, fees and customs, as amended, together with the tax authorities, consists of financial management.
New organisational structure of financial management on 1. January 2012 consists of the Financial directorate of the SLOVAK republic, Criminal office of financial administration, Competence center financial operations, tax authorities, Tax office for selected tax entities, branch offices of the tax authorities, contact points of the tax authorities, customs authorities, branch offices (branch of the CA tax, the branch of the CA combined, the branch of the CA customs) and station offices.
The main mission of the FD Sr is to effectively collect and manage taxes and customs duties, i.e. also excise taxes, to fulfill the income portion of the state budget and to protect the economic interests of the state.
The statutory body of the FD SR is the president of the financial administration, appointed and dismissed by the Minister of Finance of the Slovak Republic.
The president of the financial administration is responsible to him for the activities of the entire financial administration, and hence for the activities of the FD SR, which he directs and represents in full.
Organizational structure of FD SR from 1. 1. 2012 in abbreviated form
In addition to the branches of the customs offices (38 branches) and the Stations of the customs offices (18 stations), the Excise departments (9 departments) and the legal departments (9 departments) also provide for all customs offices in the territory of the SR.

Comparison and evaluation

As part of the organisational structure of the financial administration of the SR, in 2015, in addition to the FR SR, there were 74 organizational departments with a total number of 1,300 employees; these departments manage almost 48,000 tax entities.
Within the organisational structure of the Customs administration of the CZECH republic in the 2015 administration of the excise taxes addressed in about 60 organizational departments with a total population of 1 011 employees that manage approximately 114 000 tax subjects.

Their mutual coordination and cooperation is addressed through middle and top management.

EMCS system
According to the preamble to decision no 1152/2003/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 16. June 2003, on the introduction of an electronic system for the movement and surveillance of excisable products, the goal was to introduce an electronic system for monitoring the transport of selected products to allow the obtaining on the transport of information in real time and carry out the prescribed checks, simplify the movement of goods within the Community under suspension of excise duty.
In implementing the system, member states should have allowed economic operators, in particular SMEs active in the sector, to exploit these national elements at the lowest possible cost.
Article 3 of the said decision of the EP and of the Council admits that the EMCS included in national specifications, the national databases forming part of the system and any software or equipment which a member state considers necessary to ensure the full use of the system throughout its administration.
EMCS in the Czech Republic
Development and functionality of the EMCS system
In the Czech republic the EMCS system was preceded by a system of registration of selected products (EVV), which was operated from may 2004 until the end of march 2010.
EMCS is fully operational in the Czech Republic from 1. 4. 2010 and continuously supplemented by European and national functionalities (see Annex 5).
The so-called customs module and declarant module were introduced in the Czech Republic.
The customs module contains a number of national functionalities.
In addition to the Community System, carriage under the conditional exemption scheme initiated and completed in the Czech Republic is monitored in the EMCS system in the Czech Republic.
The system provides after the approval of the notification of acceptance of the consignment to the authorised recipient for one-time adoption of automatic sending the information to the registry of tax subjects, with a consequent zneplatněním permission.
Fully is through a system of ensured administration of received and sent requests for international cooperation and spontaneous information from ELO including sending a response with an attachment in any format and ensuring the translations.
It is also possible to receive a report on the manual cessation of exports in the ECS (only the referral of the automatically created message is implemented in the EU).
Risk profiles for outgoing or incoming shipments are set according to the currently required criteria.
The EMCS will not allow e-AD or notification of admission without the competent customs authority's response to the risk profile (the risk profile cannot be ignored).
Deklarantský module is for tax entities available for free, has the form of a web application to which a user logs in the username and password (coordinates) that are assigned to it after registration at the EN of the CZECH republic.
Any act vis-à-vis the EMCS customs module shall bear a valid electronic signature in the EMCs declarant module.
Deklarantský module allows you to tax subjects direct entry of data on initiated and completed dopravách in the regime of conditional exemption from tax, and the tax bodies may not expend funds for the acquisition system.
The national functionality deklarantského module allow you to retrieve and store the data off-line (saves time for frequently used data), filling out the details of the beneficiaries on the basis of the SEED ID, and require mandatory filling in the data that are at the EU level optional (maximum data for risk analysis).
The system also allows to block in real time the provision of excise duty in the corresponding amount of taxable transactions for each consignment sent from the Czech Republic until the termination of transport.
The amount of collateral is calculated by the EMCS system automatically.
Without a sufficient amount of collateral, the EMCs declaration module is not allowed to send a draft e-AD for approval to the CU of dispatch.
Each warranty has a unique number and contains the arc of transport (including the amount of blocked collateral) for which it was used.
The tax entity can manage its guarantees directly in the declarant EMCs module, where it sees the current amount of the blocked and unblocked excise guarantee.
Expenditure on the implementation and use of the EMCS system
The development of EMCS was carried out on the basis of eight fulfilment contracts from 2006 to 2017 totalling CZK 46 791 924.60 (i.e. € 1,761 412.56) excluding VAT.
In accordance with the contracts concluded, the contractor issued invoices for a total amount of CZK 43,577,255,19 (i.e. € 1,640,401,10) excluding VAT from 2006 to the end of 2015.
During the period under review, expenditure of CZK 14,545,454 excluding VAT (i.e. €547,438,99) was spent on the EMCS upgrade.
The amount spent on the upgrade of EMCS in the audited period and converted on one transport inserted into the EMCS is on average 16,49 € (i.e. 0,62 €), without a national transport makes these expenses in recalculation on one transport between the CZECH republic and the EU member states 24,40 € (i.e. 0,92 €).
EMCs technical support was implemented on the basis of four fulfilment contracts from 2011 to 2017.
By the end of 2015, the total amount of technical support of CZK 7,499,675 (i.e. € 281,389,77) including Value Added Tax was invoiced.
The average amount of technical support spent since 2011 per transport entered into the EMCS since 2010 is CZK 6.18 (i.e. €0.23).
The invoices for development and technical support concerned the national solution and the development of the EVV application already operated by DGC before the EMCS system itself.
The invoices were paid in the framework of programming funding from national sources.
Technical support is invoiced as part of the supply services also to other applications that the Customs administration of the CZECH republic, the supplier provides.
EMCS in SR
The EMCS is an electronic system operated by EU member states to monitor the movement of excise goods between member states under a conditional exemption scheme.
Replace the accompanying administrative document – SAD, which was used before the effectiveness of this system, and thus ensure better control and management of transport.
In SR is introduced from 1. 4. 2010 and is continuously supplemented by requirements arising from EU legislation.
A unique reference code is generated for each transport, the so-called Transport.
Arc code under which the traffic can be tracked online, i.e. in real time.
Development and functionality of the EMCS system
System EMCS ensures the receiving and sending of goods subject to excise taxes only those tax entities which are entitled to use the system, EMCS, thereby largely reduces the risk of tax evasion.
The greatest development of functionalities occurred in 2011, when the EMCS system was fully put into operation (see annex 6).
Expenditure on the implementation and use of the EMCS system
The introduction of the EMCS system was implemented as another module of the application equipment SysNeD, and therefore it is not possible on the Slovak side, to accurately determine the amount of the cost of its initial application.
Comparison and evaluation
Comparison
The aim of the EMCS was to replace the system based on the administration of transport in paper form.
Benefits of the system EMCS is a comprehensive overview of transport between member states within the EU since the announcement of the launch of transport only after its termination – a significant is the reduction of administrative costs for tax authorities and tax bodies in the processing, transmission and archiving of documents.
In the Czech Republic and in the Czech Republic, National functionality was introduced into the EMCS system allowing traffic monitoring in a conditional system between two locations in the Czech Republic or in the Czech Republic.
In addition, the automated functionality of online monitoring and guarantee of excise duty is applied in the Czech Republic.
National functionality is also established, which monitors the risk of the tax entity or transport, with the subsequent compulsory response of the tax administrator.
The SR and the Czech Republic register a comparable number of intra-EU traffic in the EMCS.
However, the expenditure incurred in the SR to upgrade this system was € 744 310.01 higher between 2012 and 2015 than in the Czech Republic.
The Sao SR received data from the Sao Sr on the upgrade of the EMCS only for the period from 2011, although this system was introduced and operated earlier.
